\section{FACTORY 1}

\subsection{Amp Showcase Presets (01A--08D)}

These presets showcase individual amp models with minimal effects, providing a direct reference for each amplifier's tonal character.


\subsubsection{01A: US Double Nrm}\hypertarget{FACTORY1-01A}{}

\noindent\textbf{Decoded:} Fender Twin Reverb (Normal Channel)

\medskip\noindent Amp showcase featuring the legendary Fender Twin Reverb's normal channel, prized for its sparkling clean headroom and lush spring reverb. A versatile studio and stage workhorse since the 1960s.

\smallskip\noindent\textbf{Recommended Pickup:} Either, Any --- \textit{Classic Fender clean---single coils are canonical but humbuckers work for a warmer voice.}

\smallskip\noindent\textit{Tempo: 120 BPM}

\smallskip
\begin{small}
\begin{longtable}{@{} l l l l @{}}
\toprule
\textbf{Category} & \textbf{Helix Name} & \textbf{Based On} & \textbf{Status} \\
\midrule
\endhead
\textcolor{disabledcolor}{Wah} & \textcolor{disabledcolor}{Weeper} & \textcolor{disabledcolor}{Arbiter Cry Baby} & \textcolor{disabledcolor}{Off} \\
Utility & Volume Pedal & Volume Pedal & On \\
\textcolor{disabledcolor}{Comp} & \textcolor{disabledcolor}{Red Squeeze} & \textcolor{disabledcolor}{MXR Dyna Comp} & \textcolor{disabledcolor}{Off} \\
\textcolor{disabledcolor}{Delay} & \textcolor{disabledcolor}{Transistor Tape} & \textcolor{disabledcolor}{Maestro EP-3} & \textcolor{disabledcolor}{Off} \\
Amp & US Double Nrm & Fender Twin Reverb (Normal) & On \\
Reverb & HX Spring & Line 6 HX Spring & On \\
\textcolor{disabledcolor}{Mod} & \textcolor{disabledcolor}{Optical Trem} & \textcolor{disabledcolor}{Fender Optical Tremolo} & \textcolor{disabledcolor}{Off} \\
Cab & 2x12 Double C12N & Fender Twin (dual mic) & On \\
\bottomrule
\end{longtable}
\end{small}

\subsubsection{01B: Essex A30}\hypertarget{FACTORY1-01B}{}

\noindent\textbf{Decoded:} Vox AC-30 Top Boost

\medskip\noindent Amp showcase for the Vox AC-30 with top boost circuit, delivering the chimey, jangly British tone that defined the British Invasion and remains a staple of indie and alternative rock.

\smallskip\noindent\textbf{Recommended Pickup:} Single Coil, Bridge or Middle --- \textit{AC-30 chime is most authentic with single coils; bridge for jangle, middle for sweetness.}

\smallskip\noindent\textit{Tempo: 120 BPM}

\smallskip
\begin{small}
\begin{longtable}{@{} l l l l @{}}
\toprule
\textbf{Category} & \textbf{Helix Name} & \textbf{Based On} & \textbf{Status} \\
\midrule
\endhead
\textcolor{disabledcolor}{Wah} & \textcolor{disabledcolor}{UK Wah 846} & \textcolor{disabledcolor}{Vox V846} & \textcolor{disabledcolor}{Off} \\
Utility & Volume Pedal & Volume Pedal & On \\
\textcolor{disabledcolor}{Drive} & \textcolor{disabledcolor}{Deranged Master} & \textcolor{disabledcolor}{Dallas Rangemaster} & \textcolor{disabledcolor}{Off} \\
Amp & Essex A-30 & Vox AC-30 (Top Boost) & On \\
\textcolor{disabledcolor}{Mod} & \textcolor{disabledcolor}{60s Bias Trem} & \textcolor{disabledcolor}{Vox Bias Tremolo} & \textcolor{disabledcolor}{Off} \\
Cab & 2x12 Silver Bell & Vox Silver Bell (dual mic) & On \\
Reverb & Dynamic Room & Line 6 Dynamic Room & On \\
\bottomrule
\end{longtable}
\end{small}

\subsubsection{01C: Brit Plexi Brt}\hypertarget{FACTORY1-01C}{}

\noindent\textbf{Decoded:} Marshall Super Lead 100 (Bright)

\medskip\noindent Amp showcase for the Marshall Super Lead 100 bright channel---the quintessential rock amplifier that launched a thousand arena tours.

\smallskip\noindent\textbf{Recommended Pickup:} Humbucker, Bridge --- \textit{Plexi bright channel into a Les Paul bridge humbucker is the classic rock pairing.}

\smallskip\noindent\textit{Tempo: 120 BPM}

\smallskip
\begin{small}

\subsubsection{01D: Cali Rectifire}\hypertarget{FACTORY1-01D}{}

\noindent\textbf{Decoded:} MESA/Boogie Dual Rectifier

\medskip\noindent Amp showcase for the MESA/Boogie Dual Rectifier, the defining high-gain amp of 1990s and 2000s heavy rock, known for its thick, saturated crunch.

\smallskip\noindent\textbf{Recommended Pickup:} Humbucker, Bridge --- \textit{High-output bridge humbucker is the canonical Rectifier pairing for tight metal rhythm.}

\smallskip\noindent\textit{Tempo: 120 BPM}

\smallskip
\begin{small}
\begin{longtable}{@{} l l l l @{}}
\toprule
\textbf{Category} & \textbf{Helix Name} & \textbf{Based On} & \textbf{Status} \\
\midrule
\endhead
Drive & Horizon Drive & Horizon Devices Precision Drive & On \\
EQ & Low/High Cut & Simple Filter & On \\
Amp & Cali Rectifire & MESA/Boogie Dual Rectifier & On \\
EQ & Parametric EQ & Line 6 Parametric & On \\
Utility & Volume Pedal & Volume Pedal & On \\
Cab & 4x12 Cali V30 & MESA/Boogie V30 (dual mic) & On \\
Reverb & Dynamic Ambience & Line 6 Dynamic Ambience & On \\
\bottomrule
\end{longtable}
\end{small}

\smallskip\noindent\textbf{Recommended Pickup:} Single Coil, Neck or Middle --- \textit{The Deluxe Reverb excels with Strat-style single coils for warm, expressive breakup.}

\subsubsection{02B: A30 Fawn Nrm}\hypertarget{FACTORY1-02B}{}

\noindent\textbf{Decoded:} Vox AC-30 Fawn (Normal)

\medskip\noindent Amp showcase for the early Vox AC-30 Fawn normal channel, the warmer-voiced predecessor to the Top Boost, favored for rounder, organic overdrive.

\smallskip\noindent\textbf{Recommended Pickup:} Single Coil, Any --- \textit{The Fawn AC-30 pairs beautifully with any single coil position for vintage British warmth.}

\smallskip\noindent\textit{Tempo: 120 BPM}

\medskip\noindent Amp showcase for the Revv Generator 120's purple channel (Ch3), a modern high-gain design with tight, focused distortion popular in progressive metal.

\smallskip\noindent\textbf{Recommended Pickup:} Humbucker, Bridge --- \textit{Modern high-gain channel designed for tight bridge humbucker articulation.}

\medskip\noindent Amp showcase for the Fender Princeton Reverb, a small-combo classic beloved for its sweet breakup and onboard reverb/tremolo.

\smallskip\noindent\textbf{Recommended Pickup:} Single Coil, Neck or Middle --- \textit{The Princeton is quintessentially a single-coil amp; neck for warmth, middle for sparkle.}

\newpage
\section{Index by Recommended Pickup Configuration}
This index groups presets by their recommended pickup type and position. Recommendations are based on the canonical guitar and pickup pairings associated with each preset's target tone, artist, or genre. Bass presets are omitted.
